5. esakapadagaLa baLake 

5.1 munnOTa 
ondu  sollu  tiLisabEkAgiruva  viSayaventahadu,  illavE  adu  naDesa 
bEkAgiruva kelasaventahadu embudannu sAmAnyavAgi adara koneyalli 
baruva esakapada aDakavAgi tiLisuttade; hAgAgi, esakapadavannu sollina 
tiruLupadavendu  kareyabahudu.  adarondige  sollinalli  baruva 
bErellA  bageya  padagaLU  esakada  kuritAgi  heccina  sangatigaLannu 
tiLisuva  mUlaka  adakke  neravAguttave;  hAgAgi,  avannu  neravupada 
gaLendu kareyabahudu. 

sollugaLa  tiruLupadagaLAgi  baralu  esakapadagaLige  halavu  bageya 
padarUpagaLu  bEkAguttave;  I  padarUpagaLannu  unTumADuvudu 
hEge,  mattu  avugaLa  tayArikeyalli  entaha  sErikeya  mArpADugaLu 
naDeyuttave  embudannu  nAlkanE  pasugeyalli  vivarisalAgide.  I  pada 
rUpagaLa  baLakeya  kuritu  kelavu  heccina  vivaragaLannu  I  pasugeyalli 
koDalAguttade. 

idallade,  tiruLesakapadagaLondige 

sollugaLalli  iru,  Agu, 
bahudu,  bEku  modalAda  kelavu  bageya  neravesakapadagaLannu  baLasa 
lAguttade;  ivu  sollinalli  baruva  bEre  neravupadagaLiginta  tiruLesaka 
padagaLige  heccu  hattiradavugaLAgiruttave,  mattu  avannu  baLasiruva 
esakapadada  iTTaLa  kelavu  viSayagaLalli  padakantegaLa  iTTaLada  hAgeyE 
kANisuttade.  antaha  neravesakapadagaLa  baLakeyannU  I  pasugeyalli 
vivarisalAgide. 

5.1.1 esakapadagaLa padarUpagaLu 
tiruLesakapadagaLigU  neravesakapadagaLigU  naDuve,  avugaLigiruva  pada 
rUpagaLa maTTige, kelavu mukyavAda vyatyAsagaLive:  

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside. 

 
340 / kannaDa barahada sollarime 

tiruLesakapadagaLige  23  konerUpagaLu  mattu  13  naDurUpagaLu 
embudAgi oTTu 36 padarUpagaLive embudannu nAvu hindina pasuge 
yalli nODiruvevu; idakke badalu, neravesakapadagaLalli iru embudakke  
idakkinta  heccu  (endare  oTTu  42)  padarUpagaLive;  uLidavugaLalli 
kelavakke  hattu  padarUpagaLive,  mattu  innu  kelavakke    adakkintalU 
kaDime padarUpagaLive. 

(1) tiruLesakapadagaLa padarUpagaLu 
tiruLesakapadagaLigiruva  konerUpagaLu  tiLivurUpagaLu  (tiLisuva  rUpa 
gaLu)  mattu  arikerUpagaLu  (kelasa  mADisuva  rUpagaLu)  embudAgi 
eraDu bageyavu; tiLivurUpagaLu mumbottu mattu himbottu embu 
dAgi  eraDu  hottugaLalli  baraballuvu  (mADuttEne,  mADide); 
Adare, arikerUpagaLu hottina vyatyAsavannu tOrisuvudilla.  

ondondu  hottinallU  tiLivurUpagaLu  (1)  ADuga,  kELuga 
mattu  heratu  embudAgi  mAtige  sambandisidantaha  mUru  bageya 
vyatyAsagaLannu,  (2)  heratu  embudaralli  ganDasu,  hengasu  mattu 
uLike  embudAgi  mUru  bageya  gurtada  vyatyAsagaLannu,  mattu  (3) 
I  ellA  kaDegaLallU  OreNike  mattu  halaveNike  embudAgi  eraDu 
bageya  eNikeya  vyatyAsagaLannu  tOrisuttave;  Adare  halaveNikeyalli 
ganDasu  mattu  hengasu  embavugaLa  naDuvina  vyatyAsa  illavAguttade 
(ivugaLa kuritu heccina vivaragaLannu 4nE pasugeyalli koDalAgide). 

hAgAgi, ondondu hottinallU tiruLesakapadagaLige oTTu ombattu 
rUpagaLu  doreyuttave.  ettugegAgi,  bare  tiruLesakapadakke  mumbotti 
nalli doreyuva ombattu rUpagaLannu keLage koDalAgide:

342 / kannaDa barahada sollarime 

Adare,  iru  padakke  allagaLeyuva  naDurUpagaLilla;  antaha  naDu 
rUpagaLu  barabEkAdallella  illa  padada  illada,  illade,  illadudu, 
illadike  emba  naDurUpagaLE  baLakeyAguttave;  hAgAgi  adakke  10 
naDurUpagaLu mAtra ive (oTTu 42 padarUpagaLu). 

illa  embudannu  iru  padada  allagaLeyuva  rUpavembudAgiyU 
hELaballevu;  Adare,  uLida  neravesakapadagaLalli  heccinavakkU  alla 
gaLeyuva  huruLiruva  padagaLu  bEreyE  Agiruva  kAraNa,  illU 
averaDannu  (iru  mattu  illa  embavugaLannu)  bEre  bEre  padagaLendu 
bageyalAgide.  idallade,  cAritrikavAgiyU  iru  mattu  illa  embavu 
gaLa naDuve sambandavilla; yAkendare, avu *ir mattu *cil emba 
eraDu bEre bEre mUladrAviDa padagaLinda bandive. 

iru padavannu neravesakapadavAgi baLasidAga, illa padada naDurUpa 
gaLa  badalu  adaravE  Ada  naDurUpagaLU  baLakeyAgaballuvu: 
mADirada kelasa, hELirada mAtu; Adare, irada emba ondu parice 
rUpa mAtra intaha baLakegaLalli baruva hAge kANisuttade.  

bal, Ar mattu ol emba mUru neravesakapadagaLalli ondom 
dakkU ombattu konerUpagaLive; Adare, bEre esakapadagaLa hAge ivakke 
hottina  rUpagaLilla;  idallade,  avugaLa  I  konerUpagaLella  tiLivu 
rUpagaLu  (balle,  balla,  ballaru),  mattu  Ar  mattu  ol  padagaLa 
tiLivurUpagaLella allagaLetada rUpagaLu (mADalAre, mADalolle). 
I mUru neravesakapadagaLigU arikerUpagaLilla. 

Ar  mattu  ol  embavakke  allagaLetada  paricerUpa  (tinnalArada, 
tinnalollada), allagaLetada jODisuva rUpa (mADalArade, mADa 
lollade),  mattu  allagaLetada  hesarurUpa  (tinnalAradudu,  tinna 
lolladudu)  embudAgi  mUru  mUru  naDurUpagaLive;  Adare, 
bal  embudakke  intaha  allagaLetada  rUpagaLilla,  balla  emba  ondu 
paricerUpa mAtra ide; mUrakkU bEDikeya rUpagaLilla. 

bEku  mattu bEDa embuvakke arikerUpa ideyallade tiLivurUpa 
villa;  bEDa  embudakke  ondu  paricerUpavU  ide  (bEDada  kelasa). 
illa  embudakke  konerUpavAgi  ondu  tiLivurUpa  mAtra  ide; 
idallade,  adakke  illada  emba  paricerUpa,  illade  emba  jODisuva 
rUpa,  illadudu  emba  udu-hesarurUpa,  mattu  illadike  emba 
ike-hesarurUpa  emba  nAlku  naDurUpagaLU  ive.  ivellavU 
allagaLeyuva rUpagaLu embudannu gamanisabahudu.  

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside. 

esakapadagaLa baLake / 343 

Agu pada Ayitu, Aguttade, Agadu, Agi, Agada mattu Agade 

emba Aru rUpagaLalli neravesakapadavAgi baLakeyAguttade. 

bahudu,  takkaddu,  bAradu  mattu  kUDadu  emba  uLida  nAlku 
neravesakapadagaLige  ondondu  rUpa  mAtra  ide;  ivugaLalli  koneya 
eraDu  padagaLu  allagaLeyuva  rUpadalli  mAtra  neravesakapadagaLAgi 
baLakeyAguttave, mattu modala eraDu padagaLige allagaLeyuva rUpa 
gaLilla. 

5.1.2 kelavu vyatyAsagaLu 
naDuviruva  vyatyAsagaLalli 
tiruLesakapadagaLigU 
kelavannu  mEle  koTTiruva  avugaLa  padarUpagaLannu  pariSIlisuva 
mUlaka tiLidukoLLabahudu; antaha vyatyAsagaLannu, mattu bEre kelavu 
vyatyAsagaLannu keLage paTTimADalAgide:  

neravesakapadagaLigU 

(1)  tiruLesakapadagaLellavU  heccukaDime  ondE  bageya,  mattu 
ondE  eNikeya  padarUpagaLalli  baruttave;  Adare,  neravesakapadagaLalli 
ondondakkU  ondondu  bageya,  mattu  ondondu  eNikeya  pada 
rUpagaLive.  

(2)  tiruLesakapadagaLige  allagaLeyada  rUpa  mattu  allagaLeyuva 
rUpa  embudAgi  eraDu  bageya  rUpagaLive;  hAgAgi,  avannu  I 
eraDu  huruLugaLallU  baLasalu  baruttade.  Adare,  neravesakapadagaLalli 
kelavakke  (Ar,  ol,  illa,  bEDa,  bAradu,  mattu  kUDadu  embu 
vakke) avugaLa ellA baLakegaLallU allagaLeyuva huruLide mattu innu 
kelavakke (iru, bal, bEku, takkaddu, mattu bahudu embuvakke) avu 
neravesakapadagaLAgi  bandiruvallellU  allagaLeyuva  huruLilla.  Agu 
emba ondu padakke mAtra neravesakapadavAgi baLasiruvallU I eraDu 
bageya rUpagaLive.  

neravesakapadagaLalli bEku mattu bEDa embuvannu bEDu esakapada 
dinda,  bAradu  mattu  kUDadu  embuvannu  baru  mattu  kUDu  esaka 
padagaLinda, mattu takkaddu embudannu tagu esakapadadinda paDeyaballe 
vAdarU,  neravesakapadagaLAgi  baLakeyAdAga  avakke  bEreyE  huruLu 
baruttade. (cAritrikavAgi, bahudu padavannU baru esakapadadindalEnE 
(barpudu>bappudu>bahudu) paDeyaballevu). 

(3)  mEle  sUcisida  hAge,  tiruLesakapadagaLige  mumbottu  mattu 
himbottu  embudAgi  eraDu  bageya  hottina  rUpagaLive;  Adare, 

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.

neravesakapadagaLalli  iru  embudakke  mumbottu,  Ipottu  mattu 
himbottu  embudAgi  mUru  hottina  rUpagaLive;  Agu  embudakke 
tiruLesakapadagaLa  hAge  eraDu  bageya  hottina  rUpagaLiveyAdarU, 
avugaLalli  Aguttade  mattu  Ayitu  embavugaLannu  mAtra  neravesaka 
padagaLAgi  baLasalAguttade;  uLida  neravesakapadagaLalli  yAvudakkU 
hottina rUpagaLilla. 

(4)  bal,  Ar  mattu  ol  embavu  nEravAgi  gurtada  oTTu 
gaLondige baruttave; mattu uLida neravesakapadagaLalli, iru embudannu 
horatupaDisi,  bEre  yAvudU  gurtada  oTTugaLu  koDaballa  huruLina 
tOrisuvudilla;  Aguttade,  Ayitu,  bahudu, 
vyatyAsagaLannu 
bAradu, kUDadu mattu takkaddu embavugaLalli uLikeya gurtada oTTu 
bandideyendu hELaballevAdarU, adannu illi bEre gurtada oTTugaLige 
edurAgi baLasilla embudannu gamanisabahudu (bEDa embudakke mAtra 
bEDi illavE bEDiri emba halaveNikeya rUpa ide).  

(5) tiruLesakapadagaLu bEre esakapadagaLa nAlku bageya jODisuva 
rUpagaLondigU  baraballuvu  (Odalu  banda,  Odi  banda,  OduttA 
banda,  Odade  banda);  Adare,  iru  padavannu  horatupaDisi,  uLida 
neravesakapadagaLu  mAresakada  jODisuva  rUpadondige  mAtra  bara 
balluvu  (mADaballe,  mADalolle,  mADalAre,  mADabEku, 
mADabEDa,  mADalilla,  mADakUDadu,  mADatakkaddu,  mADa 
bAradu, mADabahudu).  

idallade,  mAresakada  alu  oTTina  lu  embudu  mucculiyalli 
modalAguva  neravesakapadagaLu  sEridAga  bidduhOguttade  (mADa 
balle, mADabahudu, mADatakkaddu); intahadE sErikeya mArpADu 
mAresakada jODisuva rUpagaLannu kUDupadagaLalli baLasidAgalU naDe 
yuttade  embudannu  (3.3.1(3))ralli  nODiruvevu  (baramADu, 
uNabaDisu,  barahELu).  Adare,  mucculiyalli  modalAguva 
tiruLesakapadagaLu  sEridAga  alu  oTTina  lu  I  rIti  bidduhOguvu 
dilla (Odalu banda, tinnalu koTTe, Odalu hOguttAne). 

(6) tiruLesakapadagaLige Agisuva rUpa (mADiside, hELisuttAne)

gaLilla.  Agu  mattu  iru  padagaLige  Agisuva  rUpagaLiveyAdarU

esakapadagaLa baLake / 345 

5.1.3 esakada hottu 
esakada hottannu pattuge, iTTaLa mattu niluvu emba mUru mukya 
bagegaLalli tiLisalu baruttade:  

(1) hottina pattuge 
ondu  esaka  yAvAga  naDeyitu  illavE  naDeyuttade  embudannu 
hottina pattuge tiLisuttade; kannaDadalli I kelasavannu naDesalu eraDu 
holabugaLannu baLasalAguttade: 

(ka)  esakada  hottannu  sollina  hottige  sambandisidante  tiLisu 
vudu, mattu  
(ca) sollinalli tiLisiruva bErondu esakada hottige sambandisi 
dante tiLisuvudu.  

ivugaLalli  modalaneya  holabinalli  esakapadagaLa  hottina  kone 
rUpagaLannu  baLasalAguttade,  mattu  eraDaneya  holabinalli  esakapada 
gaLa  jODisuva  rUpagaLannu  baLasalAguttade;  I  eraDu  bageya 
rUpagaLa baLake hEge naDeyuttade embudannu keLage cuTukAgi vivarisa 
¯ÁVzÉ: 

(ka) solluhottige sambandisidante tiLisuvudu: 
esakada  hottannu  solluhottige  sambandisidante  tiLisuvudakkAgi 
kannaDadalli  esakapadagaLa  himbottina  rUpa  mattu  mumbottina  rUpa 
embudAgi  eraDu  bageya  hottina  rUpagaLannu  baLasalAguttade. 
ivugaLa  mUlaka  mukyavAgi  solluhottiginta  hinde  naDeda  esaka, 
mattu  adara  baLika  naDeyuva  esaka  embudAgi  solluhottigU 
esakahottigU  naDuviruva  eraDu  bageya  hottina  pattugegaLannu 
tiLisalAguttade.  ettugegAgi,  keLage  koTTiruva  sollugaLannu  gamanisa 
bahudu:  

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.

(2) hottina iTTaLa 
ondu esaka yAvAga naDeyitu illavE naDeyuttade embudAgi adara 
hottannu  bErondu  esakada  hottinondige  sambandisuva  badalu, 
adakke  hottina  maTTige  entaha  iTTaLa  ide  embudannU  tiLisaballevu; 
kannaDadalli idakkAgi eraDu bageya holabugaLannu baLasalAguttade:  

(ka) esakapadagaLa Aykeya mUlakavEnE namage bEkAgiruvantaha 
hottina iTTaLavannu tiLisuvudu ondu holabu; mattu  
(ca) esakapadada jODisuva rUpagaLondige iru padavannu nera 
vesakapadavAgi  baLasuva  mUlaka  namage  bEkAgiruva  hottina

5.2 hottina pattuge 

mEle (5.1.3)ralli vivarisida hAge, esakada hottannu ADugana illavE 
bareyuvavana  hottinondige  (solluhottinondige)  sambandisuvudu, 
mattu  sollinallEnE  tiLisiruva  bErondu  esakada  hottinondige 
sambandisuvudu  embudAgi  kannaDada  sollugaLalli  eraDu  bageya 
hottina pattugegaLannu tiLisalAguttade.  

ivugaLalli  modalanE  bageya  pattugeyannu  tiLisalu  esakapadada 
mumbottu  mattu  himbottugaLemba  eraDu  bageya  konerUpagaLannu 
baLasalAguttade  (bareyuttAre,  baredaru),  mattu  eraDanE  bageya 
pattugeyannu tiLisalu bErondu esakavannu tiLisuva padada modalesaka, 
mAresaka  mattu  oDanesakagaLemba  mUru  bageya  naDurUpagaLannu 
(jODisuva  rUpagaLannu)  baLasalAguttade  (koTTu  banda,  koDalu 
banda, koDuttA banda). 

esakapadagaLa  I  eraDu  bageya  rUpagaLa  mUlaka  mAtravallade, 
pariceyannu  tiLisuva  naDurUpagaLa  mUlaka  (bareyuva,  bareda), 
mattu  avugaLa  udu-hesarurUpagaLa  mUlakavU  esakagaLa  hottina 
pattugeyannu tiLisalu baruttade (bareyuvudu, baredudu).

divasa SeTTaru angaDibAgilannu tegeyadE irabahudu, illavE Avattu 
SeTTaru  tIrihOgi,  munde  avara  angaDiya  bAgilannu  tereyadE 
irabahudu).  intaha  baLakeya  hottannu  tiLisuvalli  esakada 
hottinondige  adara  aLaviyannU  tiLisalAguttade  embudannu  munde 
5.6ralli nODaliruvevu. 

mEle (2)ralli vivarisidantaha anisu, kELisu, eTaku, nOyu 
modalAdavugaLigiruva  Ipottina  huruLu  intaha  baLakeya  huruLige 
badalAgi  baruttade;  hAgAgi,  adannu  baLakeya  huruLina  innondu 
rUpa embudAgiyU tiLiyabahudu.

kANisuva  hAge  varNisabEkAdAga,  himbottina  esakarUpagaLa  badalu

5.3.2 konegoLLuva iTTaLa 
konegoLLuva iTTaLadalli iru padada heccina padarUpagaLannU baLasalu 
baruttade;  ike-hesarupadavannu  mAtra  idaralli  baLasalu  baruva  hAge 
kANisuvudilla.

5.3.3 toDaguva iTTaLa 
toDaguva  hottina  iTTaLavannu  tiLisalu,  tiruLesakapadada  mAresakada 
jODisuva rUpadondige iru padada padarUpagaLannu baLasalAguttade; 
Adare,  I  iTTaLada  baLakeyalli  halavu  kaTTupADugaLive.  ettugegAgi, 
iru  padada  mumbottina  konerUpagaLalli,  uLikegurtada  OreNikeya 
rUpa  mAtra  I  iTTaLadalli  baruttade,  mattu  adU  baLakeya 
huruLinalli mAtra baruttade.  

idallade,  iru  padada  arike  rUpagaLalli  yAvudU  idarondige 

baruva hAge kANisuvudilla. 

idara  baLika  iru  padada  naDurUpagaLalli  jODisuva  rUpagaLa 

baLakeyU tumbA kaDime.  

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.

5.4.3 esakada iTTaLagaLannu mArpaDisuvudu 
esakapadagaLu tiLisuva esakada iTTaLavannu avugaLondige baruva hesaru 
kantegaLu  illavE  paricenuDitagaLu  svalpamaTTige  mArpaDisaballuvu; 
avugaLondige  bEre  kelavu  esakapadagaLannu  sErisi  kUDupadagaLAgi 
mArpaDisuva  mUlakavU  avu  tiLisuva  esakada  iTTaLadalli  mArpADu 
gaLannu unTumADalu baruttade. 

(1) hesarupadagaLa baLake: 
sAguvesakavannu  tiLisuva  esakapadadondige  ondu  kanDitavAda  guri 
yannu  tiLisuva  hesarukanteyannu  baLasi,  adu  tiLisuva  esakakkondu 
elle dorakuva hAge mADalu baruttade. idannu keLagina sollugaLalli 
kANabahudu: 

(28ka)  avanu bareyuttidda. 
(28ca)  avanu ondu kate bareyuttidda. 

bareyuvudu  embudakke  mugitAya  illavE  koneyillavAdarU 
ondu  kate  bareyuvudu  embudakke  ondu  koneyide;  bareyalu 
horaTiruva  kateyannu  baredAdAga,  A  esaka  mugiyuttade.  idallade, 
hAge mugiyuvalli varegU adannu naDesuttirabahudu, illavE adannu 
naDuvinallE nillisabahudu. 

hAgAgi, mEle koTTiruva (28ka) sollininda `avanu bareda' emba 
huruLannu  paDeyalu  baruttade;  Adare,  (28ca)  sollininda  A  rIti 
`avanu  kate  bareda'  emba  huruLannu  paDeyalu  baruvudilla.  `kate 
bareyuva'  esakakkiruva  toDagu,  munduvarisu  mattu  mugisu  emba 

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.

5.4.4 hottina iTTaLadalli mArpADugaLu 
mEle  vivarisidantaha  sAguvesaka,  caNadesaka  mattu  koneyesakagaLemba 
mUru  bageya  esakapadagaLannu  mUru  bageya  hottina  iTTaLagaLalli 
(endare,  avugaLa  jODisuva  rUpakke  iru  padavannu  sErisi  unTu 
mADiruva  sikkalu  padarUpagaLalli)  baLasidAga,  avu  tiLisuva  hottina 
iTTaLadalli kelavu mArpADugaLu kANisikoLLuttave, mattu I mArpADu 
gaLu esakapadagaLa oLa iTTaLavannu avalambisiruttave. 

(1)  I  mUru  hottina  iTTaLagaLalli  toDagike  embudu  ellA 
bageya  esakagaLigU  ondE  bageyadAgiruva  kAraNa,  adannu  tiLisuva 
hottina iTTaLadalli mUru bageya esakapadagaLU heccu kaDime ondE 
bageya  huruLugaLannu  koDuttave.  idannu  keLage  koTTiruva  sollu 
gaLalli kANabahudu: 

(34ka)  avaLu ivattu hADaliddALe. 
(34ca)  avanu kada taTTaliddAne. 
(34Ta)  avanu mane kaTTaliddAne. 

mElina sollugaLalli sAguvesaka (34ka), caNadesaka (34ca), mattu 
koneyesakagaLannu  toDagikeya  hottina  iTTaLadalli  baLasalAgiddu,  I 
mUru  bageya  padagaLU  esakavondu  solluhottina  baLika  toDaga 
lide embudannu tiLisuttave. 

(2) idakke badalu, munduvarikeya hottina iTTaLadalli I mUru 
bageya  esakapadagaLannu  baLasidAga,  bEre  bEre  bageya  huruLugaLu 
dorakuttave  embudannu  nAvu  mEleyE  nODiruvevu.  sAguvesaka 
(34ka)  munduvariyuttideyemba  huruLu,  caNadesaka  (34ca)  halavu 
bAri naDeyuttideyemba huruLu, mattu koneyesaka(34Ta)da naDuvina 
hanta naDeyuttideyemba huruLu dorakuttade. 

(35ka)  avaLu hADuttiddALe. 
(35ca)  avanu nanage hoDeyuttiddAne. 
(35Ta)  avanu ganTannu biDisuttiddAne. 

munduvarikeya  iTTaLadalli  koneyesakavannu  baLasidalli,  adu 
modalE  suruvAgittu,  Adare  konegonDiralilla  emba  huruLu  sigu 

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.

5.5 ADugana niluvu 

tiruLesakapadada  jODisuva  rUpadondige  bEku,  bahudu,  bAradu,

(1Ta)  bassu keTTirabahudu.

mElina mUru sollugaLU `bassu keTTiruva' esakavannu tiLisuttave;

rondige, I esakada kuritAgi ADugana niluvEnu embudannU bEku 
mattu bahudu emba eraDu neravesakapadagaLa mUlaka tiLisuttave.  

ivugaLalli bahudu embudakkinta bEku embudu esakada kuritAgi 
ADuganige  heccu  gaTTiyAda  arivide  embudannu  tiLisuttade.  Adare, 
(1ka)  sollu  bariya  esakavannu  tiLisuttadallade,  A  rIti  esakada 
kuritAgi ADugana niluvannu tiLisalu hOguvudilla.

sollu tiLisuva hELikeya kuritAgi avana niluvEnu embudannu tiLisu 
ttave. ettugegAgi, bassu keTTirabahudu emba sollinalli `bassu keTTide' 
emba  hELikeya  kuritAgi  ADuganige  tusu  samSayavide  embudannu 
bahudu padada baLakeya mUlaka tiLisalAgide.

gaLoLage  baruva  kAraNa,  avakke  svalpa  maTTige  sollugaLa  esakapada

nalli  konege  baruva  I  oTTu  iDI  sollu  tiLisuva  hELikege  purAve

(2Ta)  I dESadalli hOTelinallU maduveyAgabahudu.

(mADalu+balla), 

mADalAra,

418 / kannaDa barahada sollarime 

5.5.1 niluvina neravesakapadagaLu 
ADugana  niluvannu  tiLisuva  bEku,  bahudu,  bAradu,  bal,  Ar 
modalAda  nerasakapadagaLige  entaha  baLakegaLive  embudannu  keLage 
vivarisalAgide;  avu  mUru  bageya  ADugana  niluvugaLannu  hEge 
tiLisuttave  embudAgi  avu  koDaballa  huruLugaLannu  munde  vivarisa 
lAguvudu. 

(1) bEku mattu bahudu 
I  eraDu  padagaLigU  hottina  oTTugaLannAgali,  illavE  gurutina 
oTTugaLannAgali nEravAgi sErisalu baruvudilla; avu ondE rUpadalli 
baLakeyAguttave.  

bEku  embudakke  bEDa  emba  allagaLeyuva  rUpa  ide;  mattu 
adannu bEku padada hAge mAresakada jODisuva rUpada baLika baLasa 
lAguttade  (hOgabEDa,  tinnabEDa);  hIgiddarU,  adannu  arikeya 
sollugaLalli  baLasalAguttadeyallade  bEku  padada  hAge  ADugana 
niluvannu tiLisuva neravesakapadavAgi baLasuvudilla. 

(3ka)  nInu manege hOgabEku. 
(3ca)  nInu manege hOgabEDa. 

(3ka) sollannu ondu niluvina sollAgi baLasalAgide, mattu (3ca) 
vannu  ondu  arikeya  sollAgi  baLasalAgide  embudannu  illi  gamanisa 
bahudu.  (3ka)  sollinalli  `kELuganu  manege  hOguttAne'  emba 
hELikeya  kuritAgi  ADuganu  tanna  niluvannu  (arivannu)  tiLisuttiddAne; 
Adare, (3ca) sollinalli Atanu A rIti tanna niluvannu tiLisuva badalu, 
nEravAgi  `manege  hOguva  esaka'vannu  kELuganu  naDesadiruvante 
taDeyuttiddAne. 

Adare,  bEku  padakke  arivina  huruLu  mAtravallade,  ottAseya 
huruLU  sigaballadu  (5.5.2  nODi);  hAgAgi,  antaha  kelavu  baLake 
gaLalli adu arikeya huruLiruva bEDa padavannu hOluttade. 

bEDa  padakke  halaveNikeya  bEDi  illavE  bEDiri  emba  rUpavU 
ide; I viSayadallU adu bEre arikerUpagaLannu (mADu, mADi, 
mADiri, tinnu, tinni, tinniri) hOluttade embudannu gamanisabahudu. 
idakke  badalu,  bEku  padakke  intaha  halaveNikeya  rUpagaLilla.  I 

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside. 

 
esakapadagaLa baLake / 419 

viSayavU bEku mattu bEDa embavu bEre bEre iTTaLagaLalli baLake 
yAguva padagaLu embudannu bembalisuttade.  

bEku  mattu  bahudu  padagaLa  baLika  ittu  padavannu  nEravAgi 
illavE  Agu  padada  mAresakada  jODisuva  rUpada  baLika  baLasalu

mADabahudAgittu).

kuritAgi ADugana niluvu entahadu (adu ondu iruha mAtra, bEha 
valla) embudannu tiLisuva innondu angavU ide.

irisalu  baruttade:  adaralliruva  hELikeyannu  allagaLeyabahudu,

(4) Araygara kaTTale 
hELikeya  allagaLetakkU  niluvina  allagaLetakkU  naDuve  tirugumurugu 
sambanda  (mArpattuge)  ide  embudAgi  Araygaru  (tArkikaru)  hELu

ottAseya  niluvannu  tiLisuva  sollugaLu  I  kaTTalege  hondi 

koLLuvudannu keLage koTTiruva ettugeyalli kANabahudu: 

1. nIvu manege hOgabahudu = nIvu manege hOgadirabEkAgilla 
2. nIvu manege hOgabAradu = nIvu manege hOgadirabEku 
3. nIvu manege hOgabEku = nIvu manege hOgadirabAradu 
4. nIvu manege hOgabEkAgilla = nIvu manege hOgadirabahudu 

mElina  sollugaLalli,  keLage  koTTiruvantaha  huruLina  sarikatanagaLu 

kANisuttave: 

1. hELike + bahudu 
2. hELike + allagaLeda bahudu  =   allagaLeda hELike + bEku 
3. hELike + bEku 
= 
4. hELike + allagaLeda bahudu  = 

allagaLeda hELike + allagaLeda bahudu 
allagaLeda hELike + bahudu 

allagaLeda hELike + allagaLeda bEku 

=

esakapadagaLa baLake / 447 

Adare, arivina niluvannu tiLisuva kannaDada sollugaLu I Araygara 
kaTTaleyannu  baLasikoLLuva  hAge  kANisuvudilla;  idannu  keLage 
koTTiruva ettugeyalli kANabahudu: 

1. avaru manege hOgabahudu   ≠  avaru manege hOgadirabEkAgilla 
≠  avaru manege hOgadirabEku 
2. avaru manege hOgalAraru  
=  avaru manege hOgadiralAraru 
3. avaru manege hOgirabEku  
4. avaru manege hOgirabEkAgilla =  avaru manege hOgadirabahudu 

illi  tondareyEnendare,  avaru  manege  hOgadirabEku  mattu 
avaru manege hOgadirabEkAgilla emba eraDu sollugaLu arivina 
niluvannu tiLisalAravu; avu ottAseya niluvannu mAtra tiLisaballuvu. 
hAgAgi, A eraDu bageya sollugaLa maTTige Araygara kaTTalege arivina 
niluvannu tiLisuva sollugaLu hondikoLLuvudilla. 

idallade, mEle tiLisida hAge, hOgade embudakke solluhottina 
modalu  naDeyadidda  esakavannu  mAtravallade,  adara  baLika  naDeya 
diruva  esakavannu  tiLisuva  huruLU  ide.  hAgAgi,  I  eraDanE 
huruLina  maTTige  mEle  (3)  mattu  (4)ralli  koTTa  sarikatana  (=) 
sariyalla.      

illi  nAvu  gamanisabEkAgiruva  viSayavEnendare,  sollarimegaLige 
avugaLadE  Ada  kaTTalegaLiruttave,  mattu  I  kaTTalegaLu  nuDiyinda 
nuDige bErAgiruttave; avakkU Araygara kaTTalegaLigU naDuve hondike 
yAgadiruvudE heccu. hAgAgi, ondondu nuDiya sollarimeyallU 
hELike  mattu  niluvugaLannu  yAva  rItiyallella  allagaLeyalAguttade 
embudannu,  avugaLalli  baLakeyAguva  sollugaLannu  pariSIlisuva 
mUlaka, bEre bErAgi kanDukoLLabEkAguttade.

ondu sollinalli baLakeyAguva hesarupadagaLu illavE hesarukantegaLu

(1) 

rAjIva maguvige ondu gombe koTTa. 

I  (1)nE  sollina  koneyalli  bandiruva  koTTa  embudu  ondu

kante gurutisuttade. 

hesarupadagaLu  tiLisuva  I  pAngugaLigU  esakapadakkU  naDuve 
entaha pattugeyide embudannu hesarupadagaLa koneyalli baruva esaka 
pattugeya  oTTugaLu  tiLisuttave.  kannaDadalli  idakkAgi  annu,  inda,  ge 
mattu alli emba nAlku oTTugaLu baLakeyAguttave embudannu nAvu 
nAlkanE pasugeyalli (4.8.2ralli) nODiruvevu. 

ettugegAgi, mEle koTTiruva (1)nE sollinalli `koDuva esaka'da 
guri yAvudu (`koTTudu yArige') embudannu tiLisuvudakkAgi magu 
padadondige  ge  oTTu  bandide;  Adare,  esakada  IDannu  (`koTTudu 
Enannu'  embudannu)  tiLisuvudakkAgi  gombe  padadondige  yAva

oTTannu  baLasabahudu;  adare,  sAmAnyavAgi  adannu  baLasadiruvudE 
heccu;  idE  sollannu,  keLage  (1ka)dalli  kANisida  hAge,  bErondu

hesarupadakantegaLa iTTaLa / 465 

rAjuvina mane, hosa mane, doDDa mane, SAleya edurigiruva 
mane  embantaha  hesarukantegaLannu  baLasalAguttade.  ivugaLalli  mane 
emba  tiruLupadadondige  rAjuvina,  hosa,  doDDa,  SAleya 
edurigiruva embantaha kelavu neravu nuDitagaLannu baLasalAgide. 

hesarupadagaLondige  intaha  neravu  nuDitagaLannu  baLasalu  innU 
ondu kAraNavide: nAvu eSTu hesarugaLannu nenapinallirisi baLasaballevu 
embudakke  ondu  mitiyide;  rAju,  jAnaki,  heggODu  modalAda 
kelavE  kelavu  koTTahesarugaLannu  mattu  mane,  mara,  kabbiNa,  tinDi 
modalAda  kelavu  sAvira  iruvahesarugaLannu  nAvu  A  rIti 
nenapinallirisi  baLasaballevu.  Adare,  namma  gamanakke  baruva,  mattu 
hesarugaLa mUlaka sollugaLalli gurutisabEkAguva vyakti, vastu, viSaya 
modalAda pAngugaLige mitiyE illa.  

idallade,  kelavu  sandarbagaLalli  ondu  vastuvina  hesaru  namage 
tiLididdarU,  namma  kELugarige  illavE  Odugarige  adu  tiLidilladira 
bahudu,  mattu  bEre  kelavu  sandarbagaLalli  adu  namagEnE  maretu 
hOgirabahudu.  intaha  sandarbagaLallU  pAngugaLannu  gurutisuvu 
dakkAgi avugaLa hesarugaLannu mAtravE baLasuva badalu, A hesarugaLige 
kelavu  neravu  nuDitagaLannU  sErisiruva  hesarukantegaLannu  baLasa 
bEkAguttade.

barE  ondu  hesarupadada  badalu  hesarukanteyannu  baLasalu 
ivakkintalU mukyavAda kelavu kAraNagaLive. ettugegAgi, hesarupadagaLa 
eNikeyannu  sariyAgi  tiLisalu  avugaLondige  eNikepadagaLannu  baLasa 
bEkAguttade  (hattu  huDugaru,  ippattaydu  rupAyi);  avugaLa 
aLateyannu  tiLisalu  aLateya  hesarukantegaLannu  baLasabEkAguttade 
(eraDu kilO sakkare, hattu lITar tengineNNe); avugaLa jAgavannu 
tiLisalu  tOrupadagaLannu  baLasabEkAguttade  (A  huDuga,  I

6.2.2 ottehesaru mattu oTTaluhesaru

gaLondige  halaveNikeya  oTTannu  baLasalu  baruttade  (huDugaru,  hakki 
gaLu,  maragaLu,  kaNNugaLu);  Adare,  oTTaluhesarugaLondige  adannu 
baLasalu baruvudilla (*tuppagaLu, *maNNugaLu).  

idallade,  ottehesarugaLondige  eNikeya  padagaLannu  nEravAgi 
baLasalu  baruttade  (hattu  huDugaru,  nAlku  hakkigaLu);  Adare,

avugaLondige eNikeya padagaLannu baLasalu baruttade (eraDu lITar 
hAlu, mUru kilO tuppa, ondu lOTa nIru).

oTTalu padagaLu eNikeya padadondige nEravAgi baLakeyAgiruva hAge

baruttade.  maruka,  bEsara,  gOLu,  madipu  modalAda  halavAru

sErisidalli  eNisalAguva  padagaLAgibiDuttave  (mUru  lITar  eNNe, 
eraDu  kilO  beNNe);  Adare,  koTTa  hesarugaLannAgali  (*mUru 
kilO kAvEri), illavE parijillada padagaLannAgali (*mUru lITar 
maruka) A rIti mArpaDisalu baruvudilla. Adare, eNisalAgada kelavu 
padagaLannu ottAyadinda antaha baLakegaLalli toDagisalU baruttade. 

ettugegAgi,  `ondE  hesarina  mUru  mandi  huDugiyaru'  emba 
huruLinalli  mUvaru  kAvEriyaru  embudAgi  koTTahesarinondige 
eNikeya  padavannu  mattu  halaveNikeya  oTTannu  baLasalu  baruttade; 
mattu  `mUru  sandarbagaLalli  unTAgiruva  daNivugaLu'  emba  huruLi 
nalli  mUru  daNivugaLu  embudAgi  parijillada  mattu  eNisalAgada 
padadondigU avannu baLasalu baruttade. 

eNisalAgada  padagaLalli  parijillada  padagaLE  mukyavAdavugaLu. 
mEle  tiLisida  hAge,  avugaLalli  heccinavannU  esakapada  illavE  parice 
padagaLige oTTugaLannu sErisi paDeyalAgide.

EzÉ.

504 /kannaDa barahada sollarime 

lAgide.  ondu  barahadalli  heccu  illavE  kaDime  tappugaLiveyendu

I viSayadalli paTTiparice mattu hantaparicegaLa naDuveyU ondu 
mukyavAda  vyatyAsavide.  mEle  vivarisida  hAge,  paTTiparicegaLannu  avu

huLi,  kahi,  cogaru  modalAda  paricepadagaLu  rucipaTTiyalli  ondu 
OraNadalli  baruvudilla;  avannu  hEge  bEkiddarU  irisabahudu.

badigaLu mattu naDuvina jAga embavugaLilla. 

hAgAgi, hantavannu tiLisuva padagaLondige, illavE hOlikeyannu 
tiLisuva  nuDitagaLondige  baLasidAga,  paTTiparicegaLu  avu  baruva 
paTTiya  hantagaLannu  tiLisuvudilla;  idakke  badalu,  paTTiyalli  baruva 
ondondu  paricegU  ondu  mAdari  beleyiddu,  I  beleginta  heccu 
illavE kaDime bele ondu vastuvigide embudannu avu tiLisuttave. 

ettugegAgi,  tumbA  dappa  (mosaru)  embudu  teLu-dappa 
aLatepaTTiyalli  dappa  embudu  tiLisuva  hantakkintalU  mEliruva

hUgaLa  maTTigiruva  mAdari  kempiginta  heccu  kempAgiruva  hU 
embudAgi  bEreyE  ondu  bageya  huruLannu  koDuttade.  adu

antaha hantagaLE illa. 

(4) hantagaLa iTTaLa 
hesarukantegaLalli  hantaparicegaLa  baLake  hEge  naDeyuttade  embudannu

viSaya,  mattu  I  hantagaLa  beleyannu  tiLiyuvalli  baLakeyAguva 
mAdari entahadu embudu innondu viSaya.

idE rItiyalli, vastuvina hareyavannu tiLisuva paricepaTTiyalli adara 
eraDu  hantagaLannu  tiLisalu  baLakeyAguva  hosa  mattu  haLe  emba 
paricepadagaLU eduruhuruLugaLannu koDuttave.

paricepadagaLu mAtra iruttave; avugaLa innondu hantavannu (eduru 
huruLannu) tiLisalu paricepadagaLiruvudilla. ettugegAgi, oLLe, bettale, 
bOLu, jiguTu, goDDu modalAda halavu paricepadagaLige avugaLa 
aLatepaTTiyalli baruva eduruhantavannu tiLisuva paricepadavilla. 

intaha  kaDegaLalli  kelavomme  eduruhuruLugaLannu  tiLisuvudakkAgi 
esakapadagaLa  pattugerUpavannu  baLasalu  baruttade:  ettugegAgi,  oLLe-
keTTa  embavugaLalli  oLLe  embudu  paricepada;  Adare,  keTTa  embudu 
keDu  esakapadada  pattugerUpa;  innu  kelavu  kaDegaLalli  allagaLeva 
rUpagaLannU  baLasalu  baruttade:  ettugegAgi,  jigaTu  embudu  ondu 
paricepada;  Adare  adara  eduruhuruLannu  koDabEkiddalli  jigaTallada 
emba adara allagaLeyuva rUpavannu baLasalu baruttade. 

eduruhuruLina  padagaLu  ondE  aLatepaTTiyalli  baruva  kAraNa 
tumbA  hattiradavAgiyU  kANisuttave,  mattu  ondakkondu  eduru 
nilluva  huruLugaLannu  koDuva  kAraNa  tumbA  dUradavAgiyU 
kANisuttave.  hOlikeyU  irabEku,  vyatyAsavU  irabEku  embudu 
ivugaLa ondu mukya parice.

6.3.2 paricepadagaLa OraNa 
ondu  hesarupadadondige  ondakkinta  heccu  paricepadagaLannu  baLasa

gaLu modalu baruttave, mattu kaDime hesarupadagaLondige baraballavu

padadondige  baraballa  hesarupadagaLiginta  tumbA  kaDime;  hAgAgi,

baruttade,  mattu  poIli  embudu  AmEle  baruttade  (avanobba 
doDDa poIli huDuga, *avanobba poIli doDDa huDuga). 

uddagala  mattu  baNNagaLannu  tiLisuva  paricepadagaLalli  baNNavannu 
tiLisuvavu  hesarupadada  hattira  nilluttave:  cikka  biLi  gombe  embudu 
sariyAgide,  Adare  *biLi  cikka  gombe  embudu  sariyAgilla  endu 
anisuvudakke idE kAraNa. intaha bEreyU kelavu OraNagaLannu keLage 
koDalAgide; ivugaLalli modalanE kAlannalli koTTiruvavu sariyendu

sariyendu tOruvudilla.

6.3.5 hesarupadagaLa pattuge rUpada baLake 
hesarupadagaLa  haravannu  kuggisuvudakkAgi  paricepadagaLannu  baLasuva 
badalu, bErondu hesarupadada pattuge rUpavannu baLasuva holabU 
kannaDadallide.  ettugegAgi,  kallina  mane  embudaralli  kallu  padada 
pattuge  rUpavAda  kallina  embudannu  mane  padada  neravu  nuDitavAgi 
baLasalAgide, mattu adu mane padada haravannu kuggisuttade: mane pada 
gurutisaballa  pAngugaLalli  kelavannu  mAtra  kallina  mane  padakante 
gurutisaballudu.  

hesarupadada  haravannu  kuggisuva  kelasadalli  bErondu  hesarupadada 
pattuge  rUpavannu  baLasuva  I  holabu  parice  padada  baLakeyannu 
hOluttade  embudannu  gamanisabahudu:  doDDa  mane  embudaralli 
bandiruva  doDDa  paricepada  hEge  mane  padada  haravannu  kuggisu 
ttadeyO hAgeyE kallina mane embudaralli bandiruva kallina pattuge 
rUpavU mane padada haravannu kuggisuttade. 

Adare  I  eraDu  holabugaLa  naDuve  kelavu  mukyavAda  vyatyAsa 

gaLive: 

(1) sAmAnyavAgi paricepadagaLu ondu pariceyannu tiLisuttiddu, A 
pariceyannu hesarupadakke sErisuva mUlaka adara haravannu kuggisuttave; 
ettugegAgi,  kempu  paricepada ondu pAngina baNNavannu  tiLisuttade; A 
paricepadavannu  hUvu  hesarupadadondige  baLasidAga,  adu  A  hesaru 
padakkiruva  huruLige  `kempu  baNNaddu'  emba  huruLannu  sErisuttade, 
mattu A mUlaka adara huruLannu kuggisuttade. 

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.

murida embudu neravupadavAgi baLakeyAgide. 

esakapadagaLige  mumbottu  (muriyuva),  himbottu  (murida) 
mattu allagaLeta (muriyada) emba mUru bageya paricerUpagaLiddu

(ca) himbottina rUpa:  murida kOlu

gaLAgi  baLakeyAgaballuvu.  hAgAgi,  hesarukantegaLalli  neravupadagaLAgi 
baLakeyAguva  esakapadagaLa  I  paricerUpagaLu  iDI  sollannE 
tammondige taraballuvu.

6.4.2 eNikepadagaLa baLake  
pAngugaLa  eNike  ondakkinta  heccu  endiSTE  mEle  vivarisida  hala 
veNikeya  oTTu  tiLisuttade;  I  eNikeyannu  heccu  vivaravAgi  tiLisalu 
adarondige (mattu kelaveDegaLalli adakke badalu) eNikeya padagaLannu 
baLasalAguttade.  ivu  hesarupadada  modalu  baruttave  (hattu 
huDugaru, eraDu manegaLu, nUrayvattu mAvina haNNu). 

intaha  eNikeya  padagaLannu  iruva  hesarugaLondige  mAtra  baLasa 
lAguttade;  sAmAnyavAgi,  koTTahesarugaLondige  avannu  baLasalu 
baruvudilla;  Adare,  mEle  6.4.1ralli  vivarisida  hAge,  ondE 
hesariruva  halavu  pAngugaLa  kuritAgi  EnAdarU  hELabEkendiruvalli 
avugaLondigU  eNikeya  padagaLannU  baLasalu  baruttade:  I  jille 
yalli mUru heggODugaLive). 

hesarupadagaLalli ottehesaru mattu oTTaluhesaru emba bEre eraDu 
gumpugaLiddu  (6.2.2  nODi),  ivugaLalli  ottehesarugaLu  gurutisuva 
pAngugaLa  eNikeyannu  tiLisalu  avugaLondige  eNikepadagaLannu  nEra 
vAgi  baLasalAguttade;  Adare,  oTTaluhesarugaLu  gurutisuva  pAngugaLa 
eNikeyannu  tiLisabEkiddalli,  avugaLondige  eNikepadagaLannu  mAtra 
vallade aLatepadagaLannU baLasabEkAguttade.  

I vyatyAsavannu hattu rupAyi mattu ondu kilO beNNe emba 
hesarukantegaLalli  kANabahudu.  rupAyi  embudu  ottehesarAgiddu, 
adarondige hattu eNikepadavannu nEravAgi baLasalAgide; Adare, beNNe 
embudu  oTTaluhesarAgiddu,  adarondige  ondu  emba  eNikepada 
dondige  kilO  emba  aLatepadavannU  baLasabEkAgide.  yAkendare, 
oTTalupadagaLondige  eNikepadagaLannu  nEravAgi  baLasalu  baruvudilla 
(*eraDu beNNe).  

hesarupadagaLondige  eNikepadagaLannu  baLasuvalli  innU  ondu 
kaTTupADide: eNisaballa mattu eNisalAgada padagaLembudAgi hesarupada 

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.

6.4.3 aLatepadagaLa baLake 
eNikeya  padagaLannu  oTTaluhesarugaLondige  baLasabEkiddalli,  avuga 
Londige  lITar,  kilO  modalAda  aLatepadagaLannu  baLasa 
bEkAguttade  (eraDu  kilO  beNNe),  avannu  nEravAgi  oTTaluhesaru 
gaLondige  baLasalu  baruvudilla  (*eraDu  beNNe)  embudannu  mEle 
nODiruvevu;  I  aLate  padagaLu  oTTaluhesarugaLige  ellegaLannu 
odagisuttave.  

(1) aLateyannu tiLisuva intaha padagaLannu oTTalu padagaLondige 
mAtravallade,  ottepadagaLondigU  baLasalu  baruttade  (eraDu  kilO 
kittaLe haNNu, mUraDi kOlu). ivugaLalli yAva aLatepada entaha 
hesarupadadondige  baraballudu  emba  viSayadalli  kelavu  kaTTupADu 
gaLive: (eraDu lITar hAlu, eraDu kilO sakkare, nAlkaDi halige, 
*eraDu lITar halige, *nAlkaDi hAlu). 

(2) aLateyannu tiLisuvalli baLakeyAguva intaha padagaLannu mukya 
vAgi eraDu gumpugaLalli irisi hELalu baruttade: yAvudAdarondu 
aLatepaTTiya  hantagaLannu  tiLisuva  lITar,  aDi,  kilO  modalA 
davugaLadu  ondu  gumpu;  mattu,  antaha  yAvudE  ondu  aLate 
paTTigU  sambandisada  buTTi,  bogase,  lOTa,  hore  modalAdavu 
gaLadu innondu gumpu.  

aLatepaTTiya  padagaLu  avugaLa  paTTiyalliruva  halavu  hantagaLalli 
ondannu gurutisuttave (miligrAm, grAm, kilogrAm). hAgAgi, 
ellA  baLakegaLallU  avakke  ondE  aLaviyannu  tiLisuva  huruLiruttade. 
Adare,  buTTi,  cIla,  kaTTu,  hore  modalAdavugaLu  A  rIti  ondu 
aLatepaTTiyalli  bArada 
kAraNa,  avu  ondondu  baLakeyalli 
ondondu  aLaviyannu  tiLisaballuvu.  hIgiddarU,  camaca,  kap 
embantaha  kelavakke  heccukaDime  ondE  bageya  aLaviyannu  tiLisuva 
huruLu bandide.

udda paricepadadondige bandide, mattu (28ca)dalli antahadE AraDi 
padajODi ettara paricepadadondige bandide.

6.4.4 aLavi padagaLa baLake

6.4.5 eNikepadagaLa iTTaLa 
eNikepadagaLalli  Aru,  ELu,  enTu  mattu  hattu  emba  nAlku 
padagaLalli  mAtra  iTTaLavannu  kANalu  baruvudilla;  Adare,  uLida 
eNikepadagaLallella  iTTaLavannu  kANalu  baruttade.  eNikebErugaLige 
oTTugaLannu  illavE  bEre  eNikepadagaLannu  sErisi  (Or-du>ondu, 
Ir-Du>eraDu,  Ir-hattu>ippattu)  avannu  paDeyabahudu, 
illavE  eNikepadagaLige  bEre  eNikepadagaLannu  sErisi  (ippatta-
Aru>ippattAru, nUra eraDu) paDeyabahudu. ivugaLa varNaneyannu 
mUraneya pasugeyalli (3.6ralli) koDalAgide. 

(1) eNikepadagaLa  modalu  innu,  matte, magad-, mattu bEre 
emba  padagaLannu  baLasalu  baruttade.  ivugaLalli  magad-  embudu 
ondu  emba  padada  modalu  mAtra  baraballudu  (magadondu, 
*magaderaDu).  uLida  padagaLu  ellA  bageya  eNikepadagaLondigU 
baraballuvu.

6.4.6 eNikepadagaLa jAga 
sAmAnyavAgi, eNikepadagaLannu hesarupadagaLa modalu baLasalAguttade; 
Adare I kaTTalege kelavu horapaDikegaLU ive: 

(1) gurta mattu eNikegaLannu tiLisuva padarUpagaLiruva ondarinda 
aydaravaregina eNikepadagaLannu tiruLupadada modaligU  baLasabahudu, 
baLikavU baLasabahudu. 

ivugaLalli  tiruLupadada  baLika  baruva  eNikepada  tiruLupada 
gurutisuva vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLa ondu amSavannaSTE gurutisu 
ttade;  Adare,  tiruLupadada  modalu  baruva  eNikepada  adara  aLavi 
yannu tiLisuttade. I vyatyAsavannu keLagina sollugaLalli kANabahudu:

(51ca) haNNugaLeraDu koLetuhOgive. 
(52ka)  obba huDuga puNeyalli OduttiddAne. 
(52ca) huDuganobba puNeyalli OduttiddAne. 

(51ka) mattu (51ca) sollugaLeraDU `koLetu hOgiruva haNNu 
gaLa  eNike  eraDu'  embudAgi  tiLisuttave;  Adare,  ivugaLalli  (51ka) 
sollige `eraDu haNNugaLu koLetuhOgive' endiSTE huruLide; Adare, 
(51ca)  sollige  `haNNugaLalli  eraDu  koLetuhOgive,  uLidavu 
koLetilla'  emba  heccina  huruLiruva  hAge  kANisuttade.  eNikepadada 
baLika  oLagoLLuva  huruLina  U  oTTannu  sErisi,  `haNNugaLalli  eraDu' 
emba I huruLu bAradante mADalu baruttade: 

(51Ta) haNNugaLeraDU koLetuhOgive.

vyatyAsavannu kANabahudu:

(52ca) rAjuvina huDugarannu ibbarannu ellarU hogaLuttAre. 

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.

(eraDaneya padavAgi) bandide. hAgAgi, nEravAgi bandideyO, pattuge 
rUpadalli  bandideyO  embudE  I  vyatyAsavannu  illi  tiLisuttade. 
ivannu ondondAgi baLasiruvallU I vyatyAsa kANisikoLLuttade:

(69ta)  nanage aydu nANyagaLu bEkAgidduvu.

emba  aLatenuDita  tiLisuva  hantakkinta  mElina  hantadallide  embudannu

eraDu pAngugaLU ondE hantadalliveyendu tiLisiruvalli avugaLa

pAngugaLannu hesarisalAguttade (2.4.3 nODi).

padagaLigU  naDuviruva  sambandagaLu  (ka)  ondu  esakada  pAngannu 
tiLisuva  sambanda,  mattu  (ca)  ondu  pAngina  pariceyannu  tiLisuva 
sambanda  embudAgi  eraDu  mukya  bageyavAgiruttave;  ettugegAgi, 
mEle pariSIlisida hesarukanteyalli rAmu mattu kudure embavugaLu 
halavu bageya esakagaLa pAngugaLAgi baraballuvAgiddu, avugaLa naDuve 
esakagaLa pAngina sambandavideyendu hELabahudu. 

idakke  badalu,  rAmuvina  aNNa  emba  innondu  hesarukanteyalli 
bandiruva  rAmu  mattu  aNNa  emba  padagaLa  naDuve  pAngina  parice 
yannu  tiLisuva  sambandavide;  I  sambandavannu  hesarukanteya  tiruLu 
padavAda  aNNa  embudE  tiLisuttade.  I  eraDu  bageya  sambandagaLa 
naDuvina  vyatyAsavannu  keLage  koTTiruva  eraDu  sollugaLalli  kANa 
bahudu: 

(10ka)  I kudure rAjuvinadu. 
(10ca)  *I aNNa rAjuvinavanu. 

esakada  pAngannu  tiLisuva  hesarukanteyannu  (10ka)dalli  kANisi 
dantaha  sollAgi  mArpaDisalu  baruttade;  Adare,  pAngina  pariceyannu 
tiLisuva hesarukanteyannu A rIti sollAgi mArpaDisalu baruvudilla.

vAda  vyatyAsavide:  sAmAnyavAgi,  ondu  hesarukanteyalli  ondakkinta 
heccu esakada pAngannu tiLisuva pattugerUpagaLu baruvudu aparUpa. 
heccendare,  antaha  eraDu  pattugerUpagaLu  baraballuvu;  adakkinta 
heccu  pattugerUpagaLannu  baLasidalli,  hesarukante  tumbA  sikkalAgi 
kANisikoLLuttade.  ettugegAgi,  keLage  koTTiruva  sollu  mattu  hesaru 
kantegaLa jODigaLannu gamanisabahudu: 

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.

6.5.2 tiLiyaballa mattu tiLiyalAgada gurutisuvikegaLu 
kELuganige  IgAgalE  tiLidiruvantaha  (illavE  tAnu  baLasuva  nuDita 
dinda  Atanige  tiLiyabahudendu  ADuganu  Uhisaballa)  gurutisuvike 
gaLu  mattu  Atanige  tiLidillada  (illavE  tAnu  baLasuva  nuDitadinda 
Atanige  tiLiyabahudendu  ADuganu  UhisalAgada)  gurutisuvikegaLu 
embudAgi  bEre  eraDu  bageya  gurutisuvikegaLannU  hesarukantegaLa 
mUlaka naDesalAguttade.  

ivannu  (kELuganige)  tiLiyaballa  mattu  tiLiyalAgada  gurutisu 
vikegaLembudAgi  illi  hesarisalAgide.  ettugegAgi,  keLage  koTTiruva 
mUru sollugaLannu gamanisabahudu:

(23ca)  huDugaru IjADalu ondu kerege hOgiddAre. 
(23ta)  huDugaru IjADalu hosa kerege hOgiddAre. 

mAtanADuva  sandarbadalli  ADugana  mattu  kELugana  manassinalli 
ondE kere ideyAdare (avara Uralli iruvudu ondE kereyAdare), 
adannu gurutisalu, (23ka)dalli kANisida hAge, kere endiSTE hELidare 
sAkAguttade.  

idakke  badalu,  ondakkinta  heccu  (illavE  bEre  bEre)  keregaLu 
avana  manassinalli  irabahudAdare,  (23ca)dalli  kANisida  hAge, 
adarondige eNikeyannu tiLisuva ondu emba padavannu baLasabEkAgu 
ttade; illavE ADugana manassinalliruva kere yAvudembudannu, (23Ta) 
dalli  kANisida  hAge,  hosa  kerege  embudAgi  nelegoLisi  tiLisa 
bEkAguttade. 

ivugaLalli  kerege  emba  hesarupada,  mattu  hosa  kerege  emba 
hesarukantegaLu  kELuganige  tiLiyaballa  gurutisuvikeyannU,  ondu

ttave embudAgi hELabahudu.

588 /kannaDa barahada sollarime 

illi  ondu  huli  embudu  ADuganu  nODidda  ondu  nijavAda 
huliyirabahudu;  illavE  adondu  kalpita  huliyAgirabahudu, 
endare  Ata  suLLu  hELuttirabahudu;  nijakkU  Ata  Avattu  kADige 
hOgiradE iddarU mElina sollannu hELaballa. 

Adare,  kELuganu  idannella  vicArisutta  hOdalli,  ADugana  mAtu 
mundakke  hOgalAradu.  hAgAgi,  ADuganu  ondu  huli  emba 
hesarukanteya  mUlaka  ondu  pAngannu  hosadAgi  gurutisuttiruva 
hAgeyE kELuganu adannu oppikonDu, Atanu tanna mAtannu mundu 
varisalu biDabEkAguttade. 

ADugaru  tamma  sollugaLalli  intaha  halavAru  tiLiyalAgada 
pAngugaLannu  hosadAgi  gurutisuttalE  iruttAre;  mattu  avannella 
kELugaru  oppikoLLuttalU  iruttAre.  Adare,  avu  entahavirabahudu 
-  nijavO,  suLLO,  kalpitavO  embudannella  mAtu  munduvariyu 
ttiruva hAge kELugaru tAvE tIrmAnisikoLLuttalU iruttAre. 

I  viSayadalli  obbobba  kELuganu  ondondu  bageya  tIrmAnakke

kalpitavAdavugaLu embudAgi tIrmAnisabahudu.  

hIgiddarU, ondu bUta emba hesarukanteya mUlaka hosadAgi 
gurutisidudannu  AmEle  adu,  adannu  embantaha  tiLiyaballa 
gurutisuvikegaLa  mUlaka  munduvarisuvudannu  ibbarU  tamma  mAtu 
gaLalli naDesalEbEkAguttade.

6.5.3 tiLiyaballa gurutisuvikeya bagegaLu 
tAnu gurutisuva pAngu tiLiyalAgaddu, illavE hosadu embudAgi

vikeyE  iruttade.  yAkendare,  adu  nEravAgi  obba  vyakti  illavE 
ondu jAgavannu hesarisuttade, mattu A vyakti illavE jAga yAvudu 
embudannu  kELuganu  tiLidiruttAnendu  anisuvalli  mAtra  ADuganu 
adannu baLasuttAne. idannu keLagina sollugaLalli kANabahudu:

rAju  emba  koTTahesaru  yArannu  hesarisuttade  embudannu 
kELuganu  tiLidiruvalli  mAtra  (30ka)  sollannu  baLasalu  baruttade; 
idE  rItiyalli,  jarman,  kannaDa  viSvavidyAlaya,  mattu  mumbayi 
emba koTTahesarugaLa baLakeyU kELugana tiLivannu avalambiside.

598 /kannaDa barahada sollarime 

6.5.5 pAngina bageyannu gurutisuvudu 
sollugaLalli  baLakeyAguva  hesarukantegaLu  nEravAgi  ondu  pAngannu 
gurutisuttirabahudu  illave  ondu  bageya  pAngannu  gurutisuttira 
bahudu; ettugegAgi, keLage koTTiruva sollannu gamanisabahudu: 

(43)   A mudukanannu kondavanige tale sariyilla.   

(43)nE  sollannu  ADuganobbanu  eraDu  huruLugaLalli  baLasira 

bahudu:  

modalaneyadAgi,  A  mudukanannu  kondavanu  embudu  obba 
vyaktiyannu  gurutisuttiddu,  Atanu  entahavanu  embudannu  tale  sari 
yilla embudu tiLisuttirabahudu;  

eraDaneyadAgi, A mudukanannu kondavanu embudu nEravAgi 
yAvudE  obba  vyaktiyannU  gurutisadirabahudu;  `A  mudukanannu 
kolluvantaha kelasavannu naDesidavanu' embudAgi ondu bageya vyakti 
yannaSTE  adu  (43)nE  sollina  pAngAgi  baLasiddu,  `antaha  vyaktige 
talesariyilla' embudAgi tiLisuttirabahudu. I eraDaneya huruLinalli 
mudukanannu  kondavanu  emba  hesarukanteyannu  baLasuvAga, 
ADugana manassinalli yAvobba vyaktiyU iruvudilla.  

nijakkU  I  eraDanE  baLakeyalli  A  mudukanannu  kondavanu 
emba hesarukante yAva obba vyaktiyannU gurutisuvudillavAda kAraNa, 
adannu `gurutisada hesarukante' embudAgiyU kareyabahudu. 

`pAngannu  gurutisuva'  mattu  `pAngannu  gurutisada'  illavE 
`pAngina  bageyannu  gurutisuva'  I  eraDu  bageya  huruLugaLalli 
yAvudannu  ondu  sollinalli  bandiruva  hesarukante  tiLisuttade 
embudu ADuganige Enu hELabEkAgide, mattu hAge hELuvalli Atana 
uddESavEnu  embudara  mEle  avalambisiruttade.  Atanige  illavE 
Atana  kELuganige  eSTu  tiLidide,  tiLidiruva  sangati  nijavO  suLLO 
embantaha bEre yAva viSayavU illi mukyavalla. 

ettugegAgi,  obba  ADuganige  ondu  viSayada  kuritAgi  ellarigU 
anvayisuvantaha  hELikeyondannu  koDabEkendirabahudu.  hAgiddalli, 
Atanu  yAvanobba  vyaktiyannU  manassinallirisikoLLade  (mattu  hesaru 
kanteya  mUlaka  antaha  vyaktiyannu  gurutisahOgade),  tanna  hELike 
yannu koDabahudu. idannu keLagina sollinalli kANabahudu: 

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.

6.5.6 tOrupadagaLinda tiLiyada gurutisuvike 
yAru, Enu, yAvanu, yAvaLu, yAvudu, mattu eSTu emba 
tOrupadagaLannu,  mattu  eSTu,  entaha  mattu  yAva  emba 
tOrupadagaLiruva hesarukantegaLannu baLasi, tiLiyada gurutisuvikeyannu 
naDesalu  baruttade.  illi  pAngu  tiLiyadiruvudu  ADuganigallade 
kELuganigalla. ettugegAgi keLagina sollugaLannu gamanisabahudu: 

(57ka)  ninne nimmallige yAru bandiddaru? 
(57ca) nimage avaralli eSTu haNa sikkitu? 
(57Ta) avaralli kelasakkiruvavanu entaha huDuga? 
(57ta)  idannu yAva huDuganige koDabEku? 

mEle  koTTiruva  sollugaLalli  yAru,  eSTu  haNa,  entaha 
huDuga,  mattu  yAva  huDuga  embavannu  pAngugaLannu  gurutisu 
vudakkAgi baLasalAgide; Adare, avu yAva pAngugaLannu, eSTu pAngu 
gaLannu illavE entaha pAngugaLannu gurutisuttave embudu ADuganige 
tiLidilla.  kELuga  avannu  tiLidirabahudembudu  Atana  anisike;  hAgAgi, 
kELugana munde Ata mElina kELvigaLannirisiruttAne. 

intaha  kELvigaLalli  mAtravallade  bEreyU  kelavu  bageya  sollu 
gaLalli  ADuganige  tiLiyadantaha  pAngannu  gurutisuva  I  tOrupada 
gaLu baraballuvu. idallade, `illavE' emba huruLina O oTTu, mattu

sollugaLalli baLasalu baruttade.

6.6 pAngugaLannu gurutisuva bEre bagegaLu 

hesarupadagaLannu  mAtravallade,  bEreyU  kelavu  bageya  padagaLannu 
baLasi  esakagaLa  pAngugaLannu  gurutisalu  baruttade.  ADupadagaLu, 
tOrupadagaLu,  eNikepadagaLu,  esakapadagaLa  hesarurUpagaLu,  mattu 
kelavu paricepadagaLu hAgU esakapadagaLu ivugaLalli mukyavAdavugaLu.  
ivugaLalli  kelavakke  hesarupadagaLinda  bErAgiruva  avugaLadE  Ada 
kelasagaLiddu,  pAngugaLannu  gurutisuva  kelasadalli  baLakeyAdAga  avu 
halavu bagegaLalli hesarupadagaLinda bErAgi kANisikoLLuttave. 

6.6.1 ADupadagaLa baLake 
ondu  sollannu  ADuttiruva  (illavE  kELuttiruva)  vyaktiyE  adara 
pAngugaLalli  ondAgideyAdalli  adannu  tiLisalu  nAnu  mattu  nInu 

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.

avugaLa  ADuga  illavE  kELugavAgiruttade  embudannu  tiLisalu  baLake

baruttade;  Adare,  hAge  mADidAgalU  avu  nanna  mattu  ninna  emba

baruvudilla.  idallade,  ibbaru  eNikepada  mAtra  I  iTTaLadalli  bara 
balludu: 

nammibbarannu yArU kareyuvudilla. 

(9PÀ)

614 /kannaDa barahada sollarime 

6.6.2 tOrupadagaLa baLake 
pAngugaLannu  gurutisuvudakkAgi  baruva  hesarupadagaLa  jAgadalli 
avanu,  avaLu,  ivanu,  adu  modalAda  tOrupadagaLannU 
baLasalu  baruttade.  Adare,  ivu  halavu  viSayagaLalli  hesarupadagaLinda 
bErAgive, mattu ADupadagaLindalU bErAgive. 

kannaDada  tOrupadagaLallella  eraDeraDu  angagaLiruttave;  ivugaLalli 
modalaneyadu  avu  sollugaLalli  naDesabEkAgiruva  kelasa  entahadu 
embudannu  tiLisuttade,  mattu  eraDaneyadu  adara  haravu  entahadu 
embudannu tiLisuttade. 

ettugegAgi, ivanu padadalli i embudu modalaneya anga; adu 
`ADugana  hattira  iruvantahadu'  emba  huruLannu  koDuttade;  avanu 
emba  innondu  tOrupadadalli  I  angakke  badalAgi  a  emba 
bErondu  anga  bandiddu,  adu  `ADuganinda  dUra  iruvantahadu' 
emba huruLannu koDuttade. 

ivanu  padadalli  eraDaneya  angavAgi  anu  embudu  bandiddu, 
adakke  `ganDugurtada  vyakti'  emba  huruLide.  ivaLu  emba  innondu 
tOrupadadalli  I  angakke  badalAgi  aLu  emba  bErondu  anga 
bandiddu, adakke `heNNugurtada vyakti' emba huruLide.

baLakeyAgaballa  tOrupadagaLannu  keLage  koTTiruva  hAge  paTTimADa

pada ADuganige tiLiyadiruva pAngannu gurutisuttade.

takkumeya  huruLinalli  baLasalAgideyAdare,  antaha  kaDegaLalli  avannu

6.6.3 eNikepadagaLa baLake 
pAngugaLannu  gurutisuvudakkAgi  eNikepadagaLannU  baLasalu  baruttade; 
intaha  baLakegaLalli  nEravAgi  avu  tiLisuva  eNikeyannE  pAngAgi 
gurutisabahudu,  illavE  A  eNikeyiruva  vastuvannU  pAngAgi 
gurutisabahudu.  

ettugegAgi,  mUrakke  nAlkannu  sErisidare  ELAguttade  emba 
sollinalli  mUru,  nAlku  mattu  ELu  padagaLannu  nEravAgi  avu 
tiLisuva  eNikeyannu  gurutisalu  baLasalAgide.  Adare,  nAlkannu 
illirisi, mattu ondannu oLagirisi emba sollinalli nAlku mattu 
ondu  padagaLannu  A  eNikeyiruva  vastugaLannu  gurutisalu  baLasa 
¯ÁVzÉ. 

eNikeyiruva vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu gurutisuvalli ondarinda 
aydaravaregina eNikepadagaLu avugaLa gurta mattu eNikeyannu tiLisuva 
padarUpagaLalli  baLakeyAguttave;  ondu  emba  pada  OreNikeyalli 
mAtra  baraballudAgiddu,  A  eNikeya  manuSyarannu  gurutisabEkAdAga 
adu  ganDugurtada  obba(nu),  heNNugurtada  obbaLu  mattu  takkumeya 
obbaru  emba  mUru  rUpagaLalli  baruttade.  manuSyarallada  prANi, 
vastu  modalAduvannu  gurutisabEkAdAga  adu  ondu  emba  rUpa 
dallE baruttade. 

(20ka)  obbanu Urige hOgiddAne. 
(20ca)  maneyalli obbaLE iddALe. 
(20Ta)  avugaLalli ondannu mEjina mElirisi. 

uLida  eNikepadagaLalli  eraDarinda  aydaravaregina  padagaLige  mAtra 
manuSyarannu  gurutisuva  ibbaru,  mUvaru,  nAlvaru  mattu  ayvaru 
emba halaveNikeya heccina rUpagaLive: 

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.

aydakkinta  mElina  eNikepadagaLannu  mandi  illavE  jana  embuda

6.6.4 esakapadagaLa hesarurUpagaLa baLake 
esakapadagaLige  udu  mattu  ike  emba  eraDu  oTTugaLannu  sErisi 
eraDu  bageya  hesarurUpagaLannu  unTumADalu  baruttade;  ivannu 
(4.7.4)ralli  hesarurUpa-1  mattu  hesarurUpa-2  embudAgi 
hesarisalAgittu;  illi  avakke  udu-rUpa  mattu  ike-rUpa  emba 
heccu aDakavAda hesarugaLannu koDalAgide.  

udu  oTTannu  esakapadagaLa  mumbottu,  himbottu  mattu  alla 
gaLetagaLemba  mUru  bageya  paricerUpagaLigU  sErisalu  baruttade; 
hAgAgi, ondondu esakapadadindalU intaha mUru mUru hesaru 
rUpagaLannu  paDeyalu  baruttade  (mADu  -  mADuvudu,  mADi 
dudu, mADadudu).  

Adare,  ike  oTTannu  mumbottina  mattu  allagaLetada  parice 
rUpagaLige  mAtra  sErisalu  baruttade;  hAgAgi,  adannu  baLasi 
ondondu  esakapadadinda  eraDeraDu  hesarurUpagaLannu  mAtra 
paDeyalu baruttade (mADu - mADuvike, mADadike). 

I  aydu  bageya  hesarurUpagaLannU  sollugaLa  pAngugaLannu 
gurutisuva  kelasadalli  baLasalu  baruttade.  idakke  kelavu  ettugegaLannu 
keLage koDalAgide:

(27ca) avaLa hADuvikege tumbA cappALe biddide. 
(27Ta) avaLa hADadikeyinda yArU bEsarapaTTilla. 

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.

paricepada  huDuga  emba  pAngina  pariceyondannu  tiLisuva  mUlaka,

padagaLa hAgeyU kANisuttave.

paricepadagaLannu  I  rIti  nEravAgi  ondu  pAngannu  gurutisuvu

gamanisabEku.  ettugegAgi,  mEle  (31ca)dalli  bandiruva  dappa  pada 
adu tiLisuva pariceyannu gurutisuttadallade, A pariceyannu paDediruva

uddaLateyannu  tiLisuva  udda-giDDa,  dappa-teLu,  agala-sapura,

dalli baLasalAgide. 

(2)  neravu  padavAgi  baruva  paricepadavannu  nEravAgi  hesarupada 
dondige  baLasalAguttade  (ettara  gODe,  udda  hagga);  Adare, 
gurutisuva  padavAgi  bandiruva  paricepadavannu  hesarupadadondige 
baLasabEkiddalli  adakke  pattugeya  a  oTTannu  sErisabEkAguttade 
(ettarada  gODe,  uddada  hagga).  I  eraDu  bagemiÀi  baLakegaLa  naDuve 
vyatyAsavide embudannu keLage koTTiruva sollugaLalli kANabahudu: 

(41ka)  I ettara gODeginta A ettara gODe cannAgide. 
(41ca) I ettarada gODeginta A ettarada gODe cannAgide. 
(41ta)  I gODeginta A gODe cannAgide. 
(41pa) I  gODeya  ettarakkinta  A  gODeya  ettara  cannAgi 

kANisuttade. 

(41ka)dalli  ettara  paricepada  gODe  padakke  neravu  nIDuvudakkAgi 
bandiddu,  adannu  hAgeyE  yAva  badalAvaNeyU  mADade  baLasa 
lAgide;  idakke  badalu,  (41ca)dalli  adE  pada  `ettara'  pariceyannu 
gurutisuvudakkAgi  bandiddu,  adannu  gODe  padadondige  baLasalu 
adakke pattugeya a oTTannu sErisabEkAgide. 

I  eraDu  sollugaLa  naDuve  huruLinalli  vyatyAsaviruvudannu 
gamanisabahudu:  (41ka)dalli  eraDu  gODegaLannu  hOlisalAgide; 
adara  huruLu  (41ta)  sollina  huruLina  hAgeyE  ide.  Adare, 
(41ca)dalli  eraDu  ettaragaLannu  hOlisalAgide;  hAgAgi,  adara 
huruLu  (41pa)  sollina  huruLina  hAgide.  (41ca)dalli  ettara  pada 
pariceyondannu gurutisuttiruvudE I vyatyAsakke kAraNa. 

hIgiddarU,  (41ca)  sollinalli  bandiruva  I  ettarada  gODe 
mattu  A  ettarada  gODe  emba  padakantegaLalli  gODe  padavE 
gODegaLannu 
tiruLu  padavAgideyAda 
hOlisuva huruLU baraballudu. 

kAraNa,  adakke  eraDu

hesarupadakantegaLa iTTaLa / 633 

6.6.6 esakapadagaLa baLake 
halavu esakapadagaLannu avugaLalli yAva mArpADannU mADade hesaru 
padagaLAgi  baLasalu  baruttade.  ettugegAgi,  rAju  kemmida  emba 
sollinalli  kemmu  pada  ondu  esakapadavAgi  baLakeyAgide;  Adare, 
rAjuvina kemmu illivarege kELisuttade emba sollinalli adE pada 
ondu hesarupadavAgi baLakeyAgide. 

kannaDadalli  heccukaDime  160  esakapadagaLannu  I  rIti  avugaLalli 
yAva  mArpADannU  mADade  hesarupadagaLAgi  baLasalu  baruttade 
(2.4.1(16)  nODi);  Adare,  ivellavU  mUladalli  esakapadagaLE; 
hesarupadagaLAgi  baruvudu  avugaLa  ondu  heccina  baLake  endu 
hELabahudu. yAkendare, halavu viSayagaLalli avu hesarupadagaLiginta 
bErAgive. 

Adare,  I  rIti  hesarupadagaLAgi  baLakeyAguva  esakapadagaLalli 
kelavu modalanE hantada (6.2.4 nODi) pAgugaLannu gurutisuttiddu, 
avu  yAva  viSayadallU  bEre  modalanE  hantada  hesarupadagaLinda 
bErAgilla. ciguru, anTu, mare, haNNu, meTTu, uguLu modalAda 
padagaLu intahavu. 

ale, uli, aLu, nagu, guDugu, hADu, nuDi, suLi modalAda 
bEre  kelavu  padagaLu  modalanE  hantada  hesarupadagaLa  hAge 
baLakeyAguvudiddarU,  kelavu  viSayagaLalli  esakapadagaLa  pariceyannU 
uLisikonDive. 

eraDanE  hantakke  sEruva  aLalu,  kudi,  Odu,  koragu,  tappu, 
kundu,  huTTu  modalAdavu  esakapadagaLa  paricegaLannu  mElinavu 
gaLiginta heccu uLisikonDive. 

hAgAgi,  I  rIti  hesarupadagaLAgi  baLakeyAgaballa  esakapadagaLannu 
bEre bErAgi pariSIlisi, avugaLa baLakeya mEliruva kaTTupADugaLannu 
paTTimADabEkAgide. ivugaLa kuritu kelavu sangatigaLannu munde ELanE 
pasugeyalli koDalAguvudu.  

6.7 tiruLu 
I  pasugeyalli  hesarukantegaLa  iTTaLa  entahadu  embudannu  vivarisa 
lAgide.  sAmAnyavAgi,  hesarukantegaLalli  ondu  hesarupada  tiruLupada 

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside. 

 
634 /kannaDa barahada sollarime 

vAgi baruttade, mattu adarondige halavu bageya padagaLu, padarUpa 
gaLu, mattu oLasollugaLu neravu nuDitagaLAgi baruttave. 

hesarupadagaLu  gurutisabEkAgiruva  pAngina  pariceyannu  tiLisu 
vudu,  aLaviyannu  tiLisuvudu,  mattu  avannu  nelegoLisuvudu  emba 
mUru  mukya  kelasagaLannu  naDesuva  mUlaka  I  neravu  nuDitagaLu 
tiruLupadavAgi  bandiruva  hesarupadagaLige gurutisuva kelasadalli nerava 
nnodagisuttave. 

hesarupadagaLu  mAtravallade,  bEreyU  kelavu  bageya  padagaLu 
mattu  padarUpagaLu  hesarukantegaLa  tiruLupadagaLAgi  baLakeyAga 
balluvu;  ADupadagaLu,  tOrupadagaLu,  eNikepadagaLu,  esakapadagaLa 
hesarurUpagaLu,  kelavu  paricepadagaLu  mattu  esakapadagaLU  I  kelasa 
dalli baLakeyAgaballuvu. Adare, ivu hesarupadagaLinda halavu viSaya 
gaLalli  bErAgive;  avugaLa  I  baLakeyalli  halavu  heccina  kaTTupADu 
gaLive. 

idu  barahada  sollarimeyAdarU,  idaralli  AgAga  ADugaru 
yAva rItiyalli hesarupadagaLannu mattu hesarukantegaLannu baLasuttAre, 
mattu  avannu  kELugaru  hEge  tiLidukoLLuttAre  embudannu  vivarisa 
lAgide;  hesarukantegaLannu  nelegoLisuva  sandarbadalli  intaha  viSaya 
gaLannu innaSTu ALavAgi pariSIlisalAgide.  

barahakkU  mAtE  mUla  embudu  hIge  mADabEkAgiruvudakke 
ondu  kAraNa;  barahadallU  ADuga  mattu  kELugaru  AgAga  kANisi 
koLLuttAre  embudu  innondu  kAraNa.  kate,  kAdambari,  nATaka 
modalAdavugaLalli I rIti ADuga mattu kELugaru kANisikoLLuvudu 
innaSTu heccu. 

bi DA. Di. en SankarabaT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside.
